\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_af18a83214bad29e8582c7d2ac7be3f14}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiApplyPostProcessing@{aiApplyPostProcessing}}
\index{aiApplyPostProcessing@{aiApplyPostProcessing}!cimport.h@{cimport.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiApplyPostProcessing()}{aiApplyPostProcessing()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_af18a83214bad29e8582c7d2ac7be3f14} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Apply\+Post\+Processing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Scene}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apply post-\/processing to an already-\/imported scene.

This is strictly equivalent to calling \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5b07b5b6589ad33033c2d456cd95da2b}{ai\+Import\+File()}/\doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00}{ai\+Import\+File\+Ex} with the same flags. However, you can use this separate function to inspect the imported scene first to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Scene} & Scene to work on. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the post-\/processed data. Post processing is done in-\/place, meaning this is still the same \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} which you passed for p\+Scene. However, {\itshape if} post-\/processing failed, the scene could now be NULL. That\textquotesingle{}s quite a rare case, post processing steps are not really designed to \textquotesingle{}fail\textquotesingle{}. To be exact, the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410ae420ce22fbbac9d0fd21fd92f2b630fa}{ai\+Process\+\_\+\+Validate\+Data\+Structure} flag is currently the only post processing step which can actually cause the scene to be reset to NULL. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a75c5aa6027cb059e63b3dda005c9c149}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiAttachLogStream@{aiAttachLogStream}}
\index{aiAttachLogStream@{aiAttachLogStream}!cimport.h@{cimport.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiAttachLogStream()}{aiAttachLogStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a75c5aa6027cb059e63b3dda005c9c149} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} void ai\+Attach\+Log\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_log_stream}{ai\+Log\+Stream}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{stream}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Attach a custom log stream to the libraries\textquotesingle{} logging system.

Attaching a log stream can slightly reduce \doxylink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}\textquotesingle{}s overall import performance. Multiple log-\/streams can be attached. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & Describes the new log stream. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure proper destruction of the logging system, you need to manually call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a98ad05bb95e8f8157a97c133812a1597}{ai\+Detach\+Log\+Stream()} on every single log stream you attach. Alternatively (for the lazy folks) \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a8f1fe2e8ccc5f93484098114ae7071bf}{ai\+Detach\+All\+Log\+Streams} is provided. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a1c142eb7bcb709482d97a63d4ce6f809}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiCreatePropertyStore@{aiCreatePropertyStore}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a1c142eb7bcb709482d97a63d4ce6f809} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_property_store}{ai\+Property\+Store}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Create\+Property\+Store (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Create an empty property store. \doxylink{struct_property}{Property} stores are used to collect import settings. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
New property store. \doxylink{struct_property}{Property} stores need to be manually destroyed using the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a579dddd75dbba5621c235df780ffc3e6}{ai\+Release\+Property\+Store} API function.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a8f1fe2e8ccc5f93484098114ae7071bf}

Detach all active log streams from the libraries\textquotesingle{} logging system. This ensures that the logging system is terminated properly and all resources allocated by it are actually freed. If you attached a stream, don\textquotesingle{}t forget to detach it again. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Get one of the predefine log streams. This is the quick\textquotesingle{}n\textquotesingle{}easy solution to access \doxylink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}\textquotesingle{}s log system. Attaching a log stream can slightly reduce \doxylink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}\textquotesingle{}s overall import performance.

Usage is rather simple (this will stream the log to a file, named log.\+txt, and the stdout stream of the process\+:

\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5b07b5b6589ad33033c2d456cd95da2b}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiImportFile@{aiImportFile}}
\index{aiImportFile@{aiImportFile}!cimport.h@{cimport.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiImportFile()}{aiImportFile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5b07b5b6589ad33033c2d456cd95da2b} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+File}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file and returns its content.

If the call succeeds, the imported data is returned in an \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} structure. The data is intended to be read-\/only, it stays property of the ASSIMP library and will be stable until \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} is called. After you\textquotesingle{}re done with it, call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} to free the resources associated with this file. If the import fails, NULL is returned instead. Call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a512bfa5aca8613168d8c5246e09b3935}{ai\+Get\+Error\+String()} to retrieve a human-\/readable error text. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+File} & Path and filename of the file to be imported, expected to be a null-\/terminated c-\/string. NULL is not a valid value. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{fwd_8h_a0e5c49dba7ec654cdda5735347c00397}{Pointer} to the imported data or NULL if the import failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiImportFileEx@{aiImportFileEx}}
\index{aiImportFileEx@{aiImportFileEx}!cimport.h@{cimport.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiImportFileEx()}{aiImportFileEx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File\+Ex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+File}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+FS}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file using user-\/defined I/O functions and returns its content.

If the call succeeds, the imported data is returned in an \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} structure. The data is intended to be read-\/only, it stays property of the ASSIMP library and will be stable until \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} is called. After you\textquotesingle{}re done with it, call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} to free the resources associated with this file. If the import fails, NULL is returned instead. Call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a512bfa5aca8613168d8c5246e09b3935}{ai\+Get\+Error\+String()} to retrieve a human-\/readable error text. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+File} & Path and filename of the file to be imported, expected to be a null-\/terminated c-\/string. NULL is not a valid value. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. \\
\hline
{\em p\+FS} & \doxylink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO} structure. Will be used to open the model file itself and any other files the loader needs to open. Pass NULL to use the default implementation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{fwd_8h_a0e5c49dba7ec654cdda5735347c00397}{Pointer} to the imported data or NULL if the import failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Include \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}ai\+File\+IO.\+h\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} for the definition of \doxylink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO}. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a7060b00dbb8a17fa117526f9e0daa139}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiImportFileExWithProperties@{aiImportFileExWithProperties}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a7060b00dbb8a17fa117526f9e0daa139} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File\+Ex\+With\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+File}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+FS}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_property_store}{ai\+Property\+Store}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Props}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Same as \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00}{ai\+Import\+File\+Ex}, but adds an extra parameter containing importer settings.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. \\
\hline
{\em p\+FS} & \doxylink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO} structure. Will be used to open the model file itself and any other files the loader needs to open. Pass NULL to use the default implementation. \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_ae6c501bf96d364eec7105560787105ff}\index{cimport.h@{cimport.h}!aiImportFileFromMemory@{aiImportFileFromMemory}}
\index{aiImportFileFromMemory@{aiImportFileFromMemory}!cimport.h@{cimport.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiImportFileFromMemory()}{aiImportFileFromMemory()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{assimp_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_ae6c501bf96d364eec7105560787105ff} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_ab51df4230ceb602bbc1bc109c432a6a0}{C\+\_\+\+STRUCT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File\+From\+Memory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Buffer}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Length}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Hint}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file from a given memory buffer,

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, NULL is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a512bfa5aca8613168d8c5246e09b3935}{ai\+Get\+Error\+String()}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Buffer} & \doxylink{fwd_8h_a0e5c49dba7ec654cdda5735347c00397}{Pointer} to the file data \\
\hline
{\em p\+Length} & Length of p\+Buffer, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_af18a83214bad29e8582c7d2ac7be3f14}{ai\+Apply\+Post\+Processing()}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Hint} & An additional hint to the library. If this is a non empty string, the library looks for a loader to support the file extension specified by p\+Hint and passes the file to the first matching loader. If this loader is unable to completely the request, the library continues and tries to determine the file format on its own, a task that may or may not be successful. Check the return value, and you\textquotesingle{}ll know ... \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the imported data, NULL if the import failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is a straightforward way to decode models from memory buffers, but it doesn\textquotesingle{}t handle model formats that spread their data across multiple files or even directories. Examples include OBJ or MD3, which outsource parts of their material info into external scripts. If you need full functionality, provide a custom IOSystem to make \doxylink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp} find these files and use the regular \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00}{ai\+Import\+File\+Ex()}/ai\+Import\+File\+Ex\+With\+Properties() API. 
\end{DoxyNote}
